2530    memcpy(nextOid, object->oid, object->oidLen);
2531 
2532    \textcolor{comment}{//Loop through network interfaces}
2533    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(index = 1; index <= \hyperlink{net_8h_a116f850ebcb023ffa3e6b8de10c5cb35}{NET\_INTERFACE\_COUNT}; index++)
2534    \{
2535       \textcolor{comment}{//Append the instance identifier to the OID prefix}
2536       n = \textcolor{keywordtype}{object}->oidLen;
2537 
2538       \textcolor{comment}{//ipv6ScopeZoneIndexIfIndex is used as instance identifier}
2539       error = \hyperlink{mib__common_8c_aedf45951f2f23c0f1250f087a620dea5}{mibEncodeIndex}(nextOid, *nextOidLen, &n, index);
2540       \textcolor{comment}{//Any error to report?}
2541       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(error)
2542          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} error;
2543 
2544       \textcolor{comment}{//Check whether the resulting object identifier lexicographically}
2545       \textcolor{comment}{//follows the specified OID}
2546       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(\hyperlink{oid_8c_a3f24a7995a2a7aa587379ec6e1922e36}{oidComp}(nextOid, n, \hyperlink{mib__common_8h_a5d78f42b3545deb9bbd305138506c7a7}{oid}, oidLen) > 0)
2547       \{
2548          \textcolor{comment}{//Save the length of the resulting object identifier}
2549          *nextOidLen = \hyperlink{dhcpv6__common_8h_a5a648f5ec00c526b0dfa2df7a272c6c0}{n};
2550          \textcolor{comment}{//Next object found}
2551          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689cabf350750d0d4fabd8954c0f1e9bbae94}{NO\_ERROR};
2552       \}
2553    \}
2554 
2555    \textcolor{comment}{//The specified OID does not lexicographically precede the name}
2556    \textcolor{comment}{//of some object}
2557    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689ca7c3779a9c0fe7d65f66367f176dee6d7}{ERROR\_OBJECT\_NOT\_FOUND};
